      (loss_fn): MaskLoss(
        (dice): BinaryDiceLoss()
      )
    )
    (fiber_keypoint_head): FiberKeypointHead(
      (conv_trunk): Sequential(
        (0): Sequential(
          (0): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )
        (1): Sequential(
          (0): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )
        (2): Sequential(
          (0): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )
        (3): Sequential(
          (0): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )
      )
      (fc_head): Sequential(
        (0): Sequential(
          (0): Linear(in_features=50176, out_features=1024, bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )
        (1): Dropout(p=0.3, inplace=False)
        (2): Sequential(
          (0): Linear(in_features=1024, out_features=512, bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )
      )
      (predictor): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=80, bias=True)
      (loss_fn): KeypointRegressionLoss()
    )
    (fiber_width_head): FiberWidthHead(
      (head): _ScalarRegressionHead(
        (pool): AdaptiveAvgPool2d(output_size=1)
        (mlp): Sequential(
          (0): Sequential(
            (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=False)
            (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
          )
          (1): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=1, bias=True)
        )
      )
    )
    (fiber_length_head): FiberLengthHead(
      (head): _ScalarRegressionHead(
        (pool): AdaptiveAvgPool2d(output_size=1)
        (mlp): Sequential(
          (0): Sequential(
            (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=False)
            (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
          )

        )
      )
    )

        (mlp): Sequential(

        (1): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=3, bias=True)
      )
      (loss_fn): QualityLoss(
        (criterion): BCEWithLogitsLoss()
      )
    )
  )
)

          (conv2): Conv2d(
            256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False
            (norm): FrozenBatchNorm2d(num_features=256, eps=1e-05)
          )
          (conv3): Conv2d(
            256, 1024, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False
            (norm): FrozenBatchNorm2d(num_features=1024, eps=1e-05)
          )
        )
        (5): BottleneckBlock(
          (conv1): Conv2d(
            1024, 256, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False

        (0): BottleneckBlock(

      (conv_fcn7): Conv2d(512, 512, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
      (conv_fcn_relu7): ReLU()
      (conv_fcn8): Conv2d(512, 512, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
      (conv_fcn_relu8): ReLU()
      (score_lowres): ConvTranspose2d(512, 40, kernel_size=(4, 4), stride=(2, 2), padding=(1, 1))
    )
    (fiber_pooler): ROIPooler(
      (level_poolers): ModuleList(
        (0): ROIAlign(output_size=(14, 14), spatial_scale=0.25, sampling_ratio=0, aligned=True)
        (1): ROIAlign(output_size=(14, 14), spatial_scale=0.125, sampling_ratio=0, aligned=True)
        (2): ROIAlign(output_size=(14, 14), spatial_scale=0.0625, sampling_ratio=0, aligned=True)
        (3): ROIAlign(output_size=(14, 14), spatial_scale=0.03125, sampling_ratio=0, aligned=True)
      )
    )
    (fiber_mask_head): FiberMaskHead(
      (convs): Sequential(
        (0): Sequential(
          (0): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )
        (1): Sequential(
          (0): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )

          (0): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )
        (3): Sequential(
          (0): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )
      )
      (deconv): ConvTranspose2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(2, 2), stride=(2, 2))
      (predictor): Conv2d(256, 1, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
      (loss_fn): MaskLoss(
        (dice): BinaryDiceLoss()
      )
    )

      (conv_trunk): Sequential(
        (0): Sequential(
          (0): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )

        )

      (loss_fn): KeypointRegressionLoss()
    )
